name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Habitat 40 Plus King
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Other
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:This is one of my more severe reviews, and it is also one of the few criticisms of Yachen Yueju in recent years. Compared with the multiple experiences of friends and family in the past five years, it is good. However, it is precisely this comparison that makes the unpleasant experience encountered this time more prominent. After my family checked in, I would visit them every day and ask the front desk staff to help me use the elevator. This was also a common situation when I visited relatives and friends before. It was very unexpected that the service staff refused to help one day. The reason was simple. Security registration was required. It happened that I did not carry my ID card. I contacted my family through the front desk and confirmed my identity. After confirming my identity, they still refused to help. I said that my family had been staying for a week. When I visited every day, I did the same thing every day to avoid the trouble of picking up the elders. Still no result. And I was told that this was an illegal operation. I did not have more doubts about the rules and regulations, nor did I pursue the hotel for not making concessions and flexible handling. Instead, I was angry and questioned the hotel staff's unprofessional operation of the industry. We can be sure that there is no hotel in the world that "can meet all customer requirements". The difference is, when you face the guests' requirements that cannot be met, how do you deal with it? The basic principle is to establish a benign channel of understanding. For the management, its significance lies in that I always stand with my customers and work together to solve problems. When the customer's requirements are beyond the scope, it is more important to build this bridge of understanding. At this time, there are two attitude choices: 1. I can't meet your requirements because it is beyond my scope. 2. I'm sorry that I can't help you. Let's see if there are other ways to improve this situation. There is a fundamental difference between the two. The former is the executor of the rules, but cold and passive; the latter is the provider of services, gentle but active. The latter is precisely the fundamental logic of the industry. This is also the inherent reason for the differences between different hotels. Unfortunately, this time, I got the former experience.
